#	TSV Format information:
#	----------------------
#	TBID (v_www_xyz) 	: Book(v), leaf(www), recto-verso(x), line(y) and number(z)
#	TB_vol_radical (xx#yyy)	: Volume(xx) and radical number(yyy)
#	TB_radical	: Radical of Chinese character 
#	Entry		: Headword
#	Entry_type	: For details, refer to the following section
#	Entry_diff	: Differences of transliteration with other scholars
#	SYID (vwwwxyyyzz)	: Book(v), leaf(www), recto-verso(x), line(yy) and number(z)
#	YYID (Ywwxxxyy-z)	: Volume(ww), leaf(xxx), line(yy) and number(z)
#	TB_remarks	: Editor's notes
#
#	Entry_type:
#	----------
#	Group a	--- Regular headword
#	1 Regular				: 隷書掲出字 (= Regular_clerical)
#	2 Regular_seal			: 隷書掲出字 篆書併存
#
#	Group b -- Embedded headword
#	3 Embedded_clerical		: 埋字 隷書字体
#	4 Embedded_omitted		: 埋字 脱落
#	5 Embedded_seal			: 埋字 篆書字体
#
#	Group c -- Omitted headword
#	6 Omitted				: 脱字 項目全体 脱落
#	7 Omitted-regular		: 脱字 隷書掲出字 脱落
#
#	Group d -- Variant of the Songben Yupian
#	8 Songben-Yupian		: 宋本《玉篇》増補之異体字
#
#   cf. Li 2015.
#   ＊6 Omitted : 項目全体脱落
#　　　　　　　　　 《説文解字》、《玉篇》残巻・佚文、《新撰字鏡》玉篇引用部分等、本文存
#
#	Abbreviations:
# 	-------------
#	TB	: Tenrei Bansho Meigi 篆隷万象名義, Kosanji copy 高山寺本
#	YY	: Yuanben Yupian 原本玉篇, fragments of vol.8, 9, 18, 19, 22, 24 and 27
#	SY	: Songben Yupian 宋本玉篇, Zecuntang edition 澤存堂本
#
# 	白	: Shirafuji's transliteration 
# 	宮	: Miyazawa's transliteration
#	上	: Ueda's transliteration
#	呂	: Lv's transliteration
#
#	References:
#	----------
#	Shirafuji	: Shirafuji Noriyuki 白藤禮幸, An Index of Headwords in the Tenrei Bansho Meigi 掲出字索引, Materials from Ancient Glossaries in the Kosanji Temple Collection 1 高山寺古辞書資料第一, Tokyo: Uiversity of Tokyo Press 東京大学出版会, 1977.
#	Miyazawa	: Miyazawa Toshimasa 宮澤俊雅, A List of Headwords with Notes in the Tenrei Bansho Meigi 掲出字一覧表, Materials from Ancient Glossaries in the Kosanji Temple Collection 1 高山寺古辞書資料第一, Tokyo: University of Tokyo Press 東京大学出版会, 1977.
#	Ueda		: Ueda Tadashi 上田正, A Complete List of Fanqie in the Original Yupian 玉篇反切総覧, Kobe: Private edition, 1986.
#	Lv		: Lv Hao 呂浩, Zhuanli Wanxiang Mingyi: A Transliteration and Text-critical Notes 篆隸萬象名義校釋, Shanghai: Xuelin Press 學林出版社, 2007.
#   Li      : Li Yuan 李媛, Embedded and Omitted Headword: Issues Regarding Entry Counts in Tenrei-Bansho-Meigi 埋字と脱字―篆隷万象名義の掲出字数をめぐる問題―, Kuntengo to Kunten-Shiryo 訓点語と訓点資料 135: 60-78, 2015.
#
#	This work was supported by JSPS KAKENHI Grant Number 25370506, 16H03422.
#
